2. FULL SCRIPT — Auto-Batch Generator
Path tools/v4_batches/generate_safe_batches.py


#!/usr/bin/env python3
import argparse
import json
import random
import subprocess
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

# -----------------------
# CONFIG
# -----------------------

SAFE_FORMATS = [
    "standard_book",
    "seven_day_reset",
    "pocket_guide",
    "practice_anthology",
    "podcast",
    None,  # registry mode
]

BOOK_SIZES = ["short", "medium", "long"]
TEACHER_MODES = ["off", "full", "composite"]
DURATIONS = ["short", "standard", "long"]

MIN_AXES_DIFFERENCE = 4
DEFAULT_BATCH_SIZE = 6


# -----------------------
# HELPERS
# -----------------------

def rand_choice(rng, items):
    return items[rng.randrange(len(items))]


def load_personas():
    import yaml
    with open("unified_personas.yaml") as f:
        data = yaml.safe_load(f)
    return list(data["personas"].keys())


def load_topics():
    # canonical topic registry
    return [
        "anxiety",
        "stress",
        "sleep",
        "focus",
        "burnout",
        "confidence",
        "motivation",
        "overthinking",
    ]


def count_axis_differences(a: Dict, b: Dict) -> int:
    diffs = 0
    for k in a:
        if a[k] != b[k]:
            diffs += 1
    return diffs


def is_valid_transition(prev: Optional[Dict], curr: Dict) -> bool:
    if prev is None:
        return True

    if prev["format_type"] == curr["format_type"]:
        return False
    if prev["persona"] == curr["persona"]:
        return False
    if prev["chapter_count"] == curr["chapter_count"]:
        return False

    if count_axis_differences(prev, curr) < MIN_AXES_DIFFERENCE:
        return False

    return True


# -----------------------
# PLAN GENERATION
# -----------------------

def generate_plan(rng, personas, topics) -> Dict:
    format_type = rand_choice(rng, SAFE_FORMATS)

    registry_mode = format_type is None
    book_size = None if registry_mode else rand_choice(rng, BOOK_SIZES)

    persona = rand_choice(rng, personas)
    topic = rand_choice(rng, topics)

    teacher_mode = rand_choice(rng, TEACHER_MODES)
    duration = rand_choice(rng, DURATIONS)

    seed = rng.randrange(10000, 99999)

    # Approx chapter count fingerprint
    chapter_count = {
        None: rng.choice([8, 10, 12]),
        "standard_book": {"short": 6, "medium": 10, "long": 12}[book_size],
        "seven_day_reset": 7,
        "pocket_guide": 1,
        "practice_anthology": {"short": 5, "medium": 9, "long": 12}[book_size],
        "podcast": 1,
    }[format_type]

    return {
        "format_type": format_type,
        "registry_mode": registry_mode,
        "book_size": book_size,
        "persona": persona,
        "topic": topic,
        "teacher_mode": teacher_mode,
        "duration": duration,
        "seed": seed,
        "chapter_count": chapter_count,
    }


def write_plan(plan: Dict, out_path: Path):
    cmd = [
        "python3",
        "phoenix_v4/tools/generate_full_plan.py",
        "--topic", plan["topic"],
        "--persona", plan["persona"],
        "--book_seed", str(plan["seed"]),
        "--duration", plan["duration"],
        "--teacher_mode", plan["teacher_mode"],
        "--output", str(out_path),
    ]

    if plan["format_type"]:
        cmd += ["--format_type", plan["format_type"]]
        if plan["book_size"]:
            cmd += ["--book_size", plan["book_size"]]
    else:
        if plan["book_size"]:
            cmd += ["--book_size", plan["book_size"]]

    subprocess.check_call(cmd)


# -----------------------
# MAIN
# -----------------------

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--out", required=True)
    ap.add_argument("--weeks", type=int, default=1)
    ap.add_argument("--batches-per-week", type=int, default=14)
    ap.add_argument("--batch-size", type=int, default=DEFAULT_BATCH_SIZE)
    ap.add_argument("--seed", type=int, default=108)
    ap.add_argument("--max-books-per-week", type=int, default=84)
    args = ap.parse_args()

    rng = random.Random(args.seed)

    personas = load_personas()
    topics = load_topics()

    out_root = Path(args.out)
    out_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    total_books = 0

    for week in range(1, args.weeks + 1):
        week_dir = out_root / f"week_{week:02d}"
        week_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

        for b in range(1, args.batches_per_week + 1):
            batch_dir = week_dir / f"batch_{b:02d}"
            plans_dir = batch_dir / "plans"
            plans_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

            batch = []
            prev = None

            while len(batch) < args.batch_size:
                candidate = generate_plan(rng, personas, topics)
                if is_valid_transition(prev, candidate):
                    batch.append(candidate)
                    prev = candidate

            # Enforce weekly cap
            if total_books + len(batch) > args.max_books_per_week * args.weeks:
                break

            # Write plans
            for i, plan in enumerate(batch):
                plan_path = plans_dir / (
                    f"{plan['topic']}_{plan['persona']}_{plan['seed']}.yaml"
                )
                write_plan(plan, plan_path)

            # Write manifests
            with open(batch_dir / "batch_manifest.json", "w") as f:
                json.dump(batch, f, indent=2)

            with open(batch_dir / "batch_guard_report.json", "w") as f:
                json.dump({
                    "batch": f"{week_dir.name}/{batch_dir.name}",
                    "books": len(batch),
                    "status": "OK",
                }, f, indent=2)

            total_books += len(batch)

    print(f"Generated {total_books} plans safely.")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

Core generation logic (exact)


def choose_publication_mode(state):
    if state.series_remaining > 0 and state.standalone_remaining > 0:
        return rng.choice(["series", "standalone"])
    if state.series_remaining > 0:
        return "series"
    return "standalone"


Series book selection


series = rng.choice(active_series)
series_position = series.next_position()

persona = series.persona

assert any(b.mode == "series" for b in batch)

       len([b for b in batch if b.series_id])
